                                   23278              Ÿ                                                                     Ÿ
                                   23279              Ÿ  FTPREAD -- Local routine to get the next FTP control line          Ÿ
                                   23280              Ÿ    from the network path.                                           Ÿ
                                   23281              Ÿ                                                                     Ÿ
                                   23282              Ÿ    On entry:                                                        Ÿ
                                   23283              Ÿ      R1 -  "x.."   String (the first character is a code which      Ÿ
                                   23284              Ÿ                    will complete the read -- see FTP doc).          Ÿ
                                   23285              Ÿ                                                                     Ÿ
                                   23286              Ÿ    On exit, R15 (and cc):                                           Ÿ
                                   23287              Ÿ      0 - ok;  R1,R0 - data line loc, len                            Ÿ
                                   23288              Ÿ      4 - Path error (message already TSEG'd)                        Ÿ
